FORTROSE & ROSEMARKIE GOLF CLUB - LINKS GOLF SINCE 1793.

Gents Winter Sweep - Stableford Format - 5 November 2016.

Garry Cameron won the first winter sweep of the season as played in a stableford format with a points total of 39 playing from a handicap of 11. In halves of 22 and 17 points Garry won by two from his nearest challengers. Second place went to Douglas Simpson with 37 points playing off a handicap of 8 (better inward half) from John Fyfe in third who also returned the same points total. Gents 18 Hole Open - 16 October 2016.

Shaun Johnson from Muir of Ord Golf Club won the Gents 18 Hole Open Scratch Section with a gross score of 71 (better last six holes) from Allan Cameron (F & R). Shaun's scorecard included birdies at the 6th, 14th and 15th holes. The best nett score in handicap section one (0-12) was returned by Gary Moore (F & R) with a 66 playing from a handicap of 5. Second place went to Derick Newbigging (F & R) with a 67 playing from a handicap of 6. In handicap section two (13-24) the best nett score was returned by Kenny Coutts (F & R) playing from a handicap of 22 with a 66. Second place went to Keith Patience (F & R) with a 67 playing from a handicap of 16. The CSS for Home Players was 69 and for Visiting Players the CSS was 72.

Open Texas Scramble - 8 October 2016.

Ladies Holm Cup - 3 Lady Team Event - 2 August 2016.

The Ladies Holm Cup Result - 3-Lady Team Format - 2 August 2016

The Junior Club Championship Final - Scratch Section - 2 August 2016.

Jake Williamson was the winner of the Junior Club Championship scratch section for 2016 after beating Matthew Clark in the final on Tuesday. This was a closely contested match where neither player was more than one ahead for the first 15 holes. A par 4 at the 17th hole from Jake was enough to take the title with the hole being halved for a 2 & 1 victory after he won the 16th hole to move two up. Jake had birdies at the 4th, 10th and 14th holes during the match to win the Club Championship for the first time.

Golf in Scotland US Masters Pairs Texas Scramble - 21 May 2016.

Douglas Simpson and Jared Simpson (Loch Ness) won the US Masters Pairs Texas Scramble handicap section on Saturday after a suspension in play due to torrential rain with an excellent nett score of 63 playing from a 20% handicap of 3. Their scorecard included gross birdies at the 4th, 7th, 12th and 17th holes and an eagle at the 6th hole to win by 0.8 from Gary Moore and Steven Bassindale. The winning scratch score was recorded by Chris Gaittens and Mike MacDonald with a gross 64 to win by two from their nearest challengers. Their scorecard included birdies at the 1st, 3rd, 7th, 11th, 13th, 14th, 15th and 16th holes. The winners now go onto the grand final which is to be played at Pumpherston Golf Club on Saturday, 10 September 2016. There is a second qualifier at Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club on Sunday, 21 August 2016.

The Donald Ross Junior Open Tournament played at Royal Dornoch Golf Club - 10 & 11 October 2015

Congratulations go to Ben Patience from Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club in winning the Donald Ross Junior Open which was played over two days (Saturday 10th & Sunday 11th October 2015) at Royal Dornoch Golf Club.

45 players competed in the tournament (4 girls and 41 boys) and they came from as far afield as Brora in the North to Haddington in the South. One player even came all the way from Germany to play in the event. Conditions were excellent on both days for the competition with many of the players taking advantage to put in good scores and reduce their handicaps.

Playing from a handicap of 11, Ben returned a nett score of 70 round the Struie Course followed by a round of nett 66 round the Royal Dornoch Championship Course to win the Peter De Savary Trophy for the first time. Ben is the first winner representing Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club since John Fair won the competition a number of years ago.

All the first and second round scores along with the results are on the Royal Dornoch Golf Club website:-

https://www.royaldornoch.com/OpenCompetitions

CONGRATULATIONS FORTROSE & ROSEMARKIE G.C.! YOU ARE 100 YEARS OLDER THAN YOU THOUGHT YOU WERE!

This information is released by Scottish Golf History to 23 contacts in the Scottish and golf press.

Last month, in the space of 40 minutes, two previously unknown newspaper notices for Earlsferry Golf Society in 1787 and Fortrose Golf Society in 1793 were discovered.

They were found in one search of the British Newspaper Archive at the National Library of Scotland in the Caledonian Mercury which published three times a week from 1720 to 1867. They bring to 18 the number of golf clubs which have a continuous or non-continuous history dating back to the 18th century.

However, not only are these two clubs now among the oldest, but their courses probably are as well. Virtually all the oldest golf clubs moved from their original golfing grounds because of congestion or to be able to create 18-hole courses in mid/late 19th century.

Fortrose Golf Society

The Fortrose Golf Society citation is a notice of the 'general annual meeting' to be held at Williamson's Tavern with dinner at 4pm on Wednesday 3rd July 1793. It is not new news that golf was played at Fortrose at this time but this date is 95 years before the Fortrose and Rosemarkie Golf Club was instituted.

More importantly it makes it more probable that the area of play on Chanonry Ness at Fortrose extended to where today’s golfers play, over the caravan park and possibly the 6th, 7th, 8th and part of 9th holes. If so that could put Fortrose in a select group of courses played before 1800. Historical map references from that time have been accessed to show where golf would have been played and this leads down from the caravan site in Fortrose to the 6th hole. A copy of the paper from this time has been sent to me so I will get this framed and put on display in the bar/dining room area when possible.

http://www.scottishgolfhistory.org/oldest-golf-clubs-societies/1793-fortrose-golf-society-1888/

http://www.scottishgolfhistory.org/oldest-golf-sites/1702-fortrose-/

The location of Williamson’s Tavern has yet to be established and any intelligence would be much appreciated.

It was always likely that there were more old golf clubs to be re-discovered and with newly digitised newspapers and other historical material, more finds were to be expected. What was totally unexpected was that two would be found in such a short space of time, both in the same search from one newspaper, the Caledonian Mercury.

Earlsferry Golf Society The announcement for Earlsferry Golf Society appeared on 26th April 1787 calling all the members to a dinner on Tuesday 1st May 1787.

Earlsferry is today better known as Elie and it is one of only three golf courses still played which goes back to 18th century or even the 16th century (the other two being the old courses at St Andrews and Musselburgh). The existence of the Earlsferry Golf Society means that formal golf club activity there also goes back to 1787 at least. This find has enabled a fuller history of the club to be written.

http://www.scottishgolfhistory.org/oldest-golf-clubs-societies/1787-earlsferry-golf-society/

http://www.scottishgolfhistory.org/oldest-golf-courses/1812-elie-and-earlsferry/

More details of the other 18 x 18th century golf clubs are given here.

http://www.scottishgolfhistory.org/news/eighteen-18th-golf-clubs/

Haggs Castle Golf Club are the Highland Heroes in TSG Club Championship Final - 20 September 2015.

Haggs Castle savoured success in the Highlands today, winning the TSG Scottish Club Championship in fine style.

The trio of Barry Hume, the Scotland internationalist, Paul Gault and Craig Morrison came out on top at Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Links, as clubs from each of the SGU Area Associations chased glory.

The winning team will now represent Scotland at the European Men’s Club Trophy at Minthis Hills in Cyprus from 22 – 24 October.

Haggs posted a winning total of six-under par, five strokes clear of Hamilton with Nairn in third spot.

For the two-round stroke play event, conditions were good in the morning, before more testing weather arrived in the afternoon, especially as the wind picked up.

Gault was the leading individual player with rounds of 69 and 70, with Hume posting scores of 72 and 70 to aid their cause. Indeed, Morrison added rounds of 69 and 74 to show the consistency of the winning side.

Stewart Henderson was the leading Hamilton player, firing rounds of 68 and 72 for two under par.

To view all of the scores from the Scottish Club Championship Final please click onto the link below:-

http://www.golfbox.dk/livescoring/tour/?language=2057#/competition/178824/leaderboard

Junior Club Championship Finals - 4 August 2015.

Calum was giving Fraser one shot on the day with the players playing off a 15 and 16 handicap respectively. The final hole was halved in four shots meaning Calum won by one hole.

The Black Isle Open Foursomes - Saturday, 11 April & Sunday, 12 April 2015.

Mike MacDonald and Chris Gaittens (both members of Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club) won the 2015 Black Isle Open Foursomes Championship (Sponsored by Munro & Noble). Unfortunately the weather was not kind to anyone as part of the qualification process with high winds making play tough to say the least. The weather was a little kinder on the Sunday for the match-play stages but again the high winds were there to make it a tough test for all players involved. The pairing of Allan Cameron (F & R)and Ewan Forbes (Inverness) topped the qualification process in the scratch section followed by John Forbes (Muir of Ord) and Davie Sanderson (Inverness). The third qualifiers were Mike MacDonald (F & R) & Chris Gaittens (F & R) and the final spot went to Lewis Reid (F & R) and Peter Cameron (F & R).

Allan and Ewan went on to beat Lewis and Peter in the semi-final on the Sunday morning by the score of 4 & 3. Mike & Chris defeated John and Davie by the score of 5 & 4 to reach the final in the scratch section.

In the final Mike and Chris defeated Allan and Ewan on the last hole to win the trophy for the third time after recovering from two down with five holes to play for victory on the last green which included four 3's in the last five holes.

In the Handicap Section, Robbie Williamson (F & R) and Derick Newbigging (F & R) won the trophy for the first time after defeating Steven Sawers (Cawder) and Richard Shepherd (Turnberry) by the score of 4 & 3 in the final which is a great achievement. The pairing of Robbie and Derick reached the final after beating Kevin Fowler (F & R) and Philip Schnier (F & R) on the last hole. In the other semi-final Stephen and Richard defeated David Lackie (F & R) and Ian Morrison (F & R) by 4 & 3.

Thank you to all of the players who took part in the Open and thank you to all of the helpers with starting and board duties covered throughout the weekend!

FORTROSE & ROSEMARKIE – The Black Isle Open Foursomes – Sponsored by Munro & Noble – Solicitors & Estate Agents (Inverness) – Scratch Qualifiers – A. Cameron (F & R) & E. Forbes (Inverness) 148 (72/76); J. Forbes (Muir of Ord) & Davie Sanderson (Inverness) 154 (72/82) M. MacDonald (F & R) & C. Gaittens (F & R) 155 (74/81); L. Reid (F & R) & P. Cameron (F & R) 157 (81/75);

Handicap Qualifiers – D. Lackie (F & R) & I. Morrison (F & R) (12) 143 (65/78); R. Williamson (F & R) & D. Newbigging (F & R) (17) 152 (76/76); K. Fowler (F & R) & P. Schnier (F & R) (6) 152 (73/79) S. Sawers (Cawder) & R. Shepherd (Turnberry) (8.5) 153 (75.5/77.5).

Best Nett Score outside of the Qualifiers – J. Jack (F & R) & R. MacLeman (F & R) (11.5) 72.5.

Match-Play Stages – Scratch Semi-Finals – A. Cameron (F & R) & E. Forbes (Inverness) beat L. Reid (F & R) & P. Cameron (F & R) 4 & 3; M. MacDonald (F & R) & C. Gaittens (F & R) beat J. Forbes (Muir of Ord) & D. Sanderson (Inverness) 5 & 4;

Final – M. MacDonald (F & R) and C. Gaittens (F & R) beat A. Cameron (F & R) & E. Forbes (Inverness) by one hole.

Handicap Semi-Finals – S. Sawers (Cawder) & R. Shepherd (Turnberry) beat D. Lackie (F & R) & I. Morrison (F & R) 4 & 3; R. Williamson (F & R) & D. Newbigging (F & R) beat K. Fowler (F & R) & P. Schnier (F & R) by one hole;

Final - R. Williamson (F & R) & D. Newbigging (F & R) beat S. Sawers (Cawder) & R. Shepherd (Turnberry) 4 & 3.

Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club Represented at the Ryder Cup - September 2014.

ClubGolfers at the Ryder Cup - 24 September 2014

Friendship Cup Leaderboard at Gleneagles - 24 September 2014

The finest young golfing talent from Europe and the United States played for the Friendship Bowl at Gleneagles on Wednesday, 24 September 2014 following the conclusion of the 2014 Junior Ryder Cup at Blairgowrie.

The 12 European juniors and their 12 American counterparts were split into six teams of two girls and two boys - one each from Europe and the United States. Each team was named after the finalists at the recent Scottish Golf Awards Ceremony and included Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club where we won the Junior Club of the Year Award in February of this year.

The Friendship Bowl was a chance to showcase the combined skills from both teams on the setting of The 2014 Ryder Cup, and it also gave the young players the opportunity to meet their golfing idols.

The Junior Ryder Cup has been the platform from which a number of successful professional careers have been built and began in 1997, two years after the idea came about at an exhibition match featuring European youngsters against a team from Central New York PGA Section.

Sergio Garcia was part of the 1995 team, Rory McIlroy played in the 2004 team and Suzann Pettersen participated in the 1997 and 1999 teams before becoming Norway’s top female golfer and playing in five Solheim Cups.

Other notable names to have played in a Junior Ryder Cup are Englishman Oliver Fisher, Italian Matteo Manassero and American Hunter Mahan, who was part of the victorious United States Team in 2008.

The contest celebrates the progress and hard work taking place at the grass roots level of golf, which helps talented young players develop into national team amateurs and some even to The Ryder Cup itself, as Garcia, McIlroy and Mahan have done.

As you can see from the picture/link at the top, Fortrose & Rosemarkie finished a creditable five under par over 9 holes. Alistair Tait and Malcolm McArthur (coaches), Ben Patience and Mac Campbell (Juniors) walked the fairways with their team at Gleneagles that very day (pictures below). Two of our other Junior ClubGolf members in Coinneach MacLeod and Rognvald MacLeod (also on a link at the top) were also in attendance and had a great day.

Mac Campbell & Ben Patience at the Ryder Cup - 24 September 2014

Fortrose & Rosemarkie win 20-Hole Northern Counties Cup Final - September 2014

Fortrose and Rosemarkie Golf Club beat Inverness Golf Club at the 20th hole in the final of the Northern Counties Cup men's double club foursomes tournament at Tain Golf Club on Saturday. Fortrose's Allan Cameron and his nephew Lewis Reid, the second couple, were six ahead of Inverness's Bryan Fotheringham and David Joel after nine holes but they were brought back to only four after 15 holes. At the same stage the Fortrose & Rosemarkie first pair, Mike MacDonald and Chris Gaittens, were three down to the Inverness first pair of John Forbes and David Sanderson (the same first pair when Inverness won at Tain in 2008).

When still four down Fotheringham and Joel surprisingly offered 8 foot putts for halves on the 16th green and it backfired when Fotheringham bunkered his tee shot to the 17th green to go five down and the 114 year old trophy looked lost in normal time however, Cameron went into the water hazard from the 18th tee. Although Reid played from it out it still took them four to reach the green and give a hole back to finish four up after 18.

With the Fortrose first pair also finding rough from the final tee, Inverness's Forbes and Joel also won the 18th hole to level the game at +4 and -4. Fotheringham and Joel had a chance to win the first extra hole but they missed their putt from 25 feet while Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club’s second pair of Cameron and Reid then had a chance to win the match but they missed from three feet after the first pair had halved in four after playing the 19th hole.

At the second extra hole, both the first pairings missed the green with their second shots. Mike MacDonald then pitched stiff from 30 feet away which left Inverness a tricky 6ft putt for a half, which they missed giving Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club the edge. After the Inverness second string of Fotheringham and Joel missed the green Reid hit his second shot to 15 feet, setting up the overall victory for Fortrose and Rosemarkie with a two putt par.

In the morning semi-finals, Nairn Dunbar, conquerors of title favourites Newmachar, winners of the trophy three times out of the previous four years, were beaten by Inverness by two holes. Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club proceeded to beat Tain Golf Club by four holes in the other semi-final. Fortrose and Rosemarkie won the Northern Counties Cup in 2002 and again in 2006. Allan Cameron was in the Inverness team that won six years ago at Tain. He has now moved his home club handicap back to his home village and as such plays for Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club.

Mike MacDonald is the Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club Secretary and a key player in his Club's last two Northern Counties Cup wins in 2002 at Tain and 2006 at Royal Aberdeen. The third win for Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club within 12 years has capped a fine year for the club. Just a week or so ago Mike MacDonald and the Match & Handicap Convener, John Jack won the Belhaven Best Captain's & Secretaries National Grand Final at Crail Golfing Society with better ball score of 64.

Fortrose and Rosemarkie Golf Club on Fire to Capture Belhaven Title in the Captains & Secretaries Grand Final at Crail Golf Society - 9 September 2014.

Fortrose and Rosemarkie Golf Club's pairing of Mike MacDonald and John Jack produced a superb better-ball score of 63 (9 under par) to storm to a four-shot victory in today’s Belhaven Best Captains & Secretaries Championship final at Crail’s Craighead Links.

MacDonald, the Club Secretary and Jack, the match and handicap convener, dovetailed to perfection as the Highland club took the title for the first time, finishing four shots clear of the Turnhouse duo of Douglas Sime and Lindsay Gordon, who combined for a net 67.

Strathaven took third place with a 68, edging out former champions Duddingston courtesy of the better inward half, on a glorious sunny and calm day in the East Neuk of Fife, with the speedy greens of the Craighead course proving a testing challenge for the field.

Scratch player MacDonald, playing in his fourth final, attributed his team’s success to consistency from both players throughout the round:

“We gelled really well out there today and it helped having a practice round yesterday to get to know the course. We were both in play on nearly every hole so we gave ourselves good chances, and I managed to knock in quite a few birdies.

“I’ve been to a few Captains and Secretaries finals so its nice to finally win one – it must be down to my partner John! We only just scraped through the regional final so probably weren’t expecting to win, but it’s great to be crowned champion of what is a great national event on a superb golf course.”

The win caps a fine year for Fortrose & Rosemarkie, who’s fantastic work in developing grass roots golf in their community earned them the title of RBS Junior Club of the Year at the Scottish Golf Awards back in February.

Belhaven’s Director of Sales, Graham Baird, said: “We are delighted to continue our sponsorship of the Belhaven Best Captains & Secretaries Championship through our SGU partnership. Golf clubs have been at the heart of the Belhaven Best success story and it’s great to support those who do so much hard work at club level by staging this championship.

“Congratulations to all 40 teams who reached the final from our hugely popular regional final series and well done to Fortrose & Rosemarkie who deservedly take the title of Scotland’s Best.”

Home CSS 70 & Visitors CSS 73.

Ross Singles win for Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club.

In a repeat of last years final Fortrose and Rosemarkie repeated their winning 3-2 scoreline of twelve months ago to hold onto the Highland Fabricators Cup in the Ross-shire Singles final at Alness Golf Club last Sunday.

Both clubs cruised through their morning semi final ties, the Tain quintet of their North District Champion Dougie Thorburn, Munro Ferries, Billy Ferries, Ross Mackenzie and Mike Sangster all won their games to oust Invergordon 5-0. The Fortrose first four of Andrew Brown, Chris Gaittens, Lewis Reid and Peter Cameron all won while senior player Robert Mackay went under to Strathpeffer's Philip Bannerman in their 4-1 result.

But Mackay was to be Fortrose & Rosemarkie's match winner in the closely fought final where the top players of each club praised the transformation brought to the Alness course by their new ex Australian green keeper Gary Urquhart whose excellent course condition was acknowledged by all.

In the final the cup holders began with Andrew Brown and Chris Gaittens both recording birdie twos on the second hole to take early leads over Dougie Thorburn and Munro Ferries respectively as Brown, after being brought back to level through nine holes, closed out the North Champion on the 17th hole where Thorburn lost a ball.

Gaittens held his one hole lead through ten holes before M Ferries got back to level with birdie on the 11th green. The tough fourteenth hole which takes its name from the Douglas Pool of the adjacent River Averon was won by Gaittens to restore his narrow one hole advantage and following two halved holes a birdie on the next par four, the 17th, secured the second point for Fortrose & Rosemarkie.

Billy Ferries got his first of many birdies on the second hole and was three ahead after five holes to complete his five and four demolition of Lewis Reid and post Tain's first point. The match result was brought level by Ross Mackenzie the hard way. He was three ahead of Fortrose & Rosemarkie's Peter Cameron with four holes to play, two of them to Cameron birdies that included one at the final hole, before MacKenzie emerged with the match levelling point at the 19th hole.

The final and deciding game involved the two oldest members of each team, Mike Sangster for Tain against Robert Mackay for Fortrose and Rosemarkie. Level after ten holes a Mackay birdie putt on the 11th green put him one in front and from a topped drive by Sangster at the next hole a two hole lead was held until the Fortrose senior ended the game with a birdie three on the penultimate hole to assure the cup returned to Fortrose and Rosemarkie for an eighth time, their first win arriving twenty years ago in 1994.

Match Results; Semi finals – Fortrose & Rosemarkie 4 Strathpeffer Spa 1. A Brown bt R Stewart 4/3. C Gaittens bt S Duff 3/2. L Reid bt A MacBean 2 up. P Cameron bt J Gordon 6/4. R Mackay lost to P Bannerman 2/1. Tain 5 Invergordon 0. D Thorburn bt D Baker 6/4. M Ferries bt K Hearton 3/2. B Ferries bt And Gilmour 4/3. R I Mackenzie bt J Fraser 4/3. M Sangster bt N Benson 5/4. Speed Golf - 16 August 2014.

Thanks must go to everyone who got up nice and early to compete in the annual speed golf challenge for the 2014 season. With 25 players turning up to play in the competition, last year's record time of 24 minutes and 15 seconds was eclipsed on what turned out to be a windy day on the links with an official time of 21 minutes and 16 seconds. Well done to everyone involved and hopefully next year with more numbers the 20 minute barrier can be beaten.

Junior Club Championship Finals Day - 9 July 2014.

Scratch Section

Euan Gill won the Junior Club Championship Scratch Section for the first time with a 5 & 3 win against Andrew Howell. In what was Euan's second consecutive scratch final, he managed to go one better this year and beat Andrew on the 15th green. Euan Gill birdied the 1st and the 10th in the final and Andrew Howell birdied the 3rd hole and the 10th hole in the match.

Handicap Section

Calum Brindle won the Junior Club Championship Handicap Section for the first time with a 3 & 2 win over Rory Brese in the final. In what was a close match all the way, Calum managed to win the 14th hole with a birdie and he then went on to win both the 15th and 16th holes to secure the win in what was his second consecutive final having lost out last year to Andrew Howell. Both players are definitely better than their handicaps currently show and there is little doubt they will improve over the next few years.

ALISTAIR TAIT WINS THE GOLF FOUNDATION’S ‘GALLACHER AWARD’

The Golf Foundation President’s Awards on Wednesday (21st of May) celebrated some of the “heroes of junior golf” who have given their time and enthusiasm to provide young people from all backgrounds and abilities with a start in the game.

Held in the perfect setting of Wentworth Club’s Ballroom, a packed audience from the world of golf heard the stories of nine award winners and their projects, featuring the volunteers, PGA Professionals, junior organisers, schoolteachers and local authority officers who all help to develop the golfers and leading players of the future.

Chairman of the Golf Foundation, Charles Harrison, gave special mention to the generosity of The European Tour and Wentworth Club for providing the stage, and also to one of the ceremony’s guests of honour, Ryder Cup player Nicolas Colsaerts, who kindly presented each of the awards on the day. Nicolas was one of the heroes on his Ryder Cup debut in 2012 as he and Lee Westwood beat Tiger Woods and Steve Stricker in the Friday fourballs, the Belgian star carding eight birdies and an eagle of his own in that match.

Charles Harrison said: “So many of us remember the wonderful effort of Nicolas at Medinah. We could wish for no better golfer to present our awards today as he and the rest of Europe’s Ryder Cup Team will have been a huge inspiration to a new generation of young golfers and also to all those who work in the sport.” Leading the ceremony, Golf Foundation Chief Executive Mike Round said: “Every year we organise this event so we can highlight the incredible work of the people at the grass roots who make it possible for children and young people to experience golf and the benefits it has to offer.

“There could not be a better time or place to do this – here at one of the most impressive golf venues in the country, which is also the home of The European Tour, one of our greatest supporters, and on the eve of the BMW PGA Championship itself.

“In the newspapers over the next few days, we will read about the incredible ability of the golfers taking part at Wentworth this week. It is however worth remembering that the efforts and achievements of our award winners are equally impressive, albeit in a different way. Without these dedicated, heroes of junior golf, many of golf’s star players would never find their game, and thousands of other young people would miss the chance to enjoy this great sport.” A number of golf’s biggest names were present to applaud the winners, many of whom are volunteers, and who all support the Foundation’s aim to make the game more accessible to children in schools, communities and golf clubs through its ‘HSBC Golf Roots’ programme.

THE ‘GALLACHER AWARD’

The Gallacher Award is for an exceptional volunteer and Alistair Tait at Fortrose and Rosemarkie Golf Club wins the accolade. Supporting the coaching there since 2005, Alistair is now Coaching Coordinator of the junior section, seeing this rising from 94 to 131 in 2013.

Alistair secured funding to develop the practice facilities and set out a three-hole mini-course on the practice ground for the younger juniors. Coaching numbers in 2013 were exceptional with 80 children signing up after Easter and a total of nine trained coaches taking regular one-hour sessions.

Attention to detail is a key. Alistair purchased and fitted mirrors to the storage shed on the practice area as a teaching aid, and painted the three covered bays himself. The club’s reputation led to a visit from the French Golf Federation to experience its methods, and the club was the first without a PGA Pro to be awarded the status of a Scottish Golf Development Centre. Mike Round said: “Teams need leaders and Fortrose and Rosemarkie’s junior programme has one of the best.”

The Black Isle Open Foursomes - Saturday, 12th April & Sunday, 13th April 2014.

Allan Cameron and Ewan Forbes (Inverness) won the Black Isle Open Foursomes Championship (Sponsored by Munro & Noble) for 2014 with an excellent showing on what turned out to be one of the toughest weekends for scoring that we are likely to see. The pairing of Allan and Ewan topped the qualification process with two very decent gross scores of 78 ahead of Mike MacDonald (F & R) & Chris Gaittens (F & R). The third qualifiers were Steven Bassindale (F & R) & Gary Moore (F & R) followed by Neil McWilliam (Elgin) and Barry Cruickshank (Spey Bay). Allan and Ewan went on to beat Neil and Barry on the Sunday morning semi-final by the score of 7 & 5. Gary & Steven then beat Mike & Chris on the 20th hole to reach their first ever final in the scratch section.

In the final Allan and Ewan defeated Gary and Steven by 2 & 1 to win the trophy for the fifth time on what turned out to be a very wet and windy afternoon not to mention the driving wind in the morning semi-final matches.

In the Handicap Section, Lewis Patience (F & R) and Ryan Keith (F & R) retained their title after defeating Robbie MacKay and Andy Gray by 3 & 2 in the final. Lewis Patience first won this trophy when playing with his brother Sandy 31 years ago so that in itself is an amazing feat. The new pairing of Robbie and Andy reached the final after beating Arthur MacArthur (F & R) and Lewis MacLeman (F & R) by the score of 3 & 2. In the other semi-final Lewis and Ryan defeated Graham Godsman (F & R) and Eric Brown (Inverness) by 4 & 3.

Thank you to all of the players who took part in the Open and just to finish 36 holes on the Saturday was a feat in itself!

Gents Winter Sweep - Stableford - 8 March 2014

RBS Junior Club of the Year - Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club.

Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club has been named the Country’s No.1 Club for young golfers after winning the 2013/14 RBS Junior Club of the Year at the 2014 Scottish Golf Awards - ClubGolfScotland.

Presented at the star-studded Hilton Glasgow event, the Black Isle Golf Club beat off stiff competition from Peebles, Prestonfield and Bathgate after a landmark 125th Anniversary year in which junior golf took centre stage.

Prestonfield coach Liz Taylor was the night's other big winner, picking up the hotly-contested RBS Volunteer of the year accolade for her dedication to developing junior golf at the Edinburgh venue.

Upon receiving the £1,500 first prize for return investment into the juniors at Fortrose & Rosemarkie, club secretary Mike MacDonald said: "I was totally unaware that we were going to win the award but to win it is just a fantastic achievement for the club.

"We've had a lot of recognition already and I think, on the back of this, we can take the club forward even more. For the coaches it means a lot as well because those are the guys that put the hard work in.

"Obviously, we had such a fantastic year last year with it being our 125th anniversary at the golf club. There was just so much going on but I think the enthusiasm of the coaches was the key thing that helped us to deliver everything we wanted to. They have given up so much of their time for the kids and our coaching is a massive thing for encouraging them to play.

"Being the 2014 RBS Junior Club of the Year will certainly help ClubGolf grow at our venue. We had 80 children taking part in ClubGolf coaching last year and we will do as much as we can to promote ourselves as the RBS Junior Club of the Year, which will hopefully encourage even more to come along in the future."

Over the course of 2013, the Highland club invested heavily in new practice facilities and coaching resources for their juniors and has experienced an increase in young members as a result, from 94 to 131, making it one of the busiest sections in the country.

Similar success was experienced at Prestonfield, where 2013/14 RBS Volunteer of the Year Liz Taylor oversaw the introduction of golf for the first time to over 100 children.

Having become the club's first ClubGolf Co-ordinator at the beginning of 2013, Liz has spearheaded the funding and construction of two brand new par-3 practice holes, delivered and organised coaching for a total of 124 children on Tuesdays, Saturdays and Sundays and even began sessions for ladies interested in taking up the game.

Delighted to be named Scotland's top golfing volunteer and receive £500 for her club, Liz said: "Winning the RBS Volunteer of the year award means that all of the hard work and effort that you put in: i.e. the admin side of it and the organisation of the classes; getting all of the coaches ready; drawing up rotas; communicating with the parents and coaches, has paid off. I put in a lot of hours but the rewards are absolutely massive and it just means the world to me. I'm delighted.

"Having 74 children joining the club in 2013 is a massive achievement for us but the most important thing is making sure the kids keep coming back. That is what makes it special for us as coaches.

"We've heard that some of them keep their golf clubs under their beds and their membership cards under their pillows because they are just so excited about ClubGolf they can hardly sleep. Things like that make this the best job in the world."

Bruce Cook, Head of Group Sponsorship at RBS, was pleased to see Scotland's top junior club and volunteer rewarded for their dedication and congratulated this year's successful candidates on their achievements.

"The 2014 Scottish Golf Awards was another great event and RBS is very proud to sponsor the Volunteer and Junior Club of the Year awards. As with our ClubGolf partnership, we think it is important to recognise the grass roots efforts that ultimately drive the future of the game.

"Both of this year's winners have shown great commitment and a collaborative spirit to grow the game. As ClubGolf continues to bring more kids into the game, we rely on individuals like Liz Taylor and those involved at Fortrose & Rosemarkie to keep it going strong."

Watching on proudly as each of the deserving RBS Awards winners was recognised in front of a 650-strong crowd, including 1995 Ryder Cup-winning Captain Bernard Gallacher, ClubGolf Manager Jackie Davidson said: "If it wasn't for our hard working clubs and dedicated volunteers, the ClubGolf programme simply couldn't exist, so I'm delighted to see Fortrose & Rosemarkie and Prestonfield's Liz Taylor recognised for their success over the last year with the 2013/14 RBS Awards.

"These awards are just a small token of our thanks for their work in introducing and retaining children in golf, which will stand their clubs in good stead for the future.

"Of course, we mustn't forget the many other applications we received in this particularly strong year. All of these together give me great confidence that golf at grass roots level in Scotland is in good hands.

"Hopefully learning more about the achievements of this year's winners can inspire even more clubs to recognise the importance of having a strong junior section and how the ClubGolf programme can help them to achieve this."

Gents Winter Sweep - Stableford - 8 February 2014

Eight in the Running for RBS Club and Volunteer Awards

ClubGolf is delighted to announce the shortlists for the 2013/14 RBS Junior Club of the Year and Volunteer of the Year Awards, featuring eight clubs and individuals who’ve made a real difference over the past 12 months.

The £1,500 first prize for RBS Junior Club of the Year will be contested between Bathgate, Fortrose & Rosemarkie, Peebles and Prestonfield after each enjoyed a landmark year in attracting youngsters to the game.

Competition in the individual category is just as strong with Dundas Parks’ Jim Cowper, Alastair Tait of Fortrose & Rosemarkie, Liz Taylor from Prestonfield and Thornton member Fraser McDonald in contention for £500 for reinvestment into their clubs, plus £100 to use personally.

The winners will be presented at the glitzy 2014 Scottish Golf Awards, alongside some of the biggest names in golf. Two representatives from each aforementioned club will attend the Hilton Glasgow on 28 February to see the victors crowned, where they will also witness Scottish Ryder Cup legend Bernard Gallacher receive a Lifetime Achievement award.

Applications for the RBS Volunteer of the Year were invited from all volunteers involved in Scottish golf, while the club prize is reserved for those clubs and facilities affiliated with ClubGolf.

ClubGolf Manager Jackie Davidson is delighted the hard work being done for junior golf at clubs and the tireless enthusiasm of Scotland’s volunteers is being recognised once again.

She said: “For everyone at ClubGolf, the RBS Awards are one of the highlights of the year as we get to see those who have put their time and effort into our programme rewarded for this terrific work.

“As always, we have had a great response across the country with many terrific stories of those doing their utmost to improve Scottish golf at the grass roots.

“Our shortlists, while not exhaustive of the great work being done, represent those clubs and individuals who have done the most to encourage participation in the game of golf and we look forward to seeing the winners crowned at the 2014 Scottish Golf Awards.”

On their backing of the 2013/14 Junior Club and Volunteer awards, RBS Group Head of Sponsorship Bruce Cook is happy to once again support the positive work being done across Scotland to preserve the health of the game.

“We really are pleased to be a part of these awards as they celebrate the foundation and future of the game,” he said. “The hard work of clubs to grow the junior game and the selfless contribution of so many volunteers across Scotland is incredibly impressive and gives us all confidence that golf in Scotland is on a positive trend.

“The pool of candidates for these awards is always strong and the selections have not been easy, but we commend all candidates and hope these awards can help the clubs achieve even more success in the years to come.”

Gents Turkey Tourney (Stableford) - Sunday, 15 December 2013.

Willie Graizer was the winner of the Gents Turkey Tourney for 2013 and as a result won the Christmas Hamper with a fantastic score of 36 points. Whilst there was little rain until later on in the round, the wind was blowing so hard that members trolleys were constantly being blown over. Long iron's and even woods were being played off the 5th tee which only measures 120 yards in length.

Willie's score included a birdie three at the 10th hole and 12 pars in halves of 16 and 20 points to win by two from his nearest challenger. With scoring so difficult for those playing on the course it was no surprise that two thirds of the field failed to get to as much as 30 points. Thankfully there were plenty of flasks on the course and a drink station at the 11th hole to keep the spirits up!

Kay Bisset returned the lowest nett score as part of the final Ladies Winter Medal for the 2013 season with a score of 81 less 14 for a nett 67. Kay's scorecard included a birdie three at the 15th hole in halves of 41 and 40 to win by one shot from Rosemary Stallard who returned a nett score of 68. Due to major bunker renovations throughout the course this medal was a reductions only competition meaning that the CSS for the day was 72 (Reductions Only).

Open Texas Scramble - Saturday 12 October 2013.

The quartet of Neil Jaffrey (F & R), Robert Gillett (F & R), C Thompson (Royal Dornoch) and G MacDonald (Inverness) won the final open competition of the 2013 season with a nett team score of 54.0 playing off an handicap of 5.0. Their card included birdies at the 1st, 4th, 5th, 8th, 9th, 10th, 14th & 17th holes and the team also eagled the 6th and 16th holes during their round. In second position were John Hearmon, Ian Duff, bob McFadyen and Tom Forbes (all Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club) with a nett score of 54.6 playing off a handicap of 4.4. In 3rd position were a team from Panmure Golf Club (G Summers, J Wallace, S Graham and D Ogilvie) with a nett team score of 56.3 playing off a handicap of 2.7. The Gents Winter Sweep - 2013/2014

THE WINTER SWEEP COMPETITIONS ARE WALK-ON THEREFORE YOU CAN CHOOSE YOUR OWN PARTNERS

  • SUNDAY, 27TH OCTOBER 2013 (STROKE PLAY)
  • SATURDAY, 9TH NOVEMBER 2013 (STABLEFORD)
  • SUNDAY, 24TH NOVEMBER 2013 (STROKE PLAY)
  • SATURDAY, 7TH DECEMBER 2013 (STABLEFORD)
  • SUNDAY, 22ND DECEMBER 2013 (STROKE PLAY)
  • SATURDAY, 11TH JANUARY 2014 (STABLEFORD)
  • SUNDAY, 26TH JANUARY 2014 (STROKE PLAY)
  • SATURDAY, 8TH FEBRUARY 2014 (STABLEFORD)
  • SUNDAY, 16TH FEBRUARY 2014 (STROKE PLAY)
  • SATURDAY, 8TH MARCH 2014 (STABLEFORD)

THE WINTER SWEEP WILL BE PLAYED FROM THE WINTER TEES AND IS NON-QUALIFYING OVER A COURSE WHICH IS NOT MEASURED. THE BEST 3 NETT SCORE AGGREGATE TOTALS FROM THE 5 STROKE-PLAY WINTER SWEEP COMPETITIONS AND THE BEST 3 POINTS TOTALS (TO FORM AN AGGREGATE) FROM THE 5 STABLEFORD WINTER SWEEP COMPETITIONS WILL DETERMINE THE WINNER/S. THE BEST SCORES FROM EACH SWEEP WILL HAVE THEIR LOYALTY CARDS CREDITED ACCORDINGLY EACH MONDAY MORNING WITH RESULTS ALSO PUBLISHED.

FOURBALLS ARE PERMITTED – BOOK OWN TIMES IN THE GOLF SHOP OR ONLINE THE ENTRY FEE PER COMPETITOR IS £2.00 [PAID IN SHOP] - [JUNIORS ENTERING MUST BE OFF A HANDICAP OF 12 OR BELOW].

Prize Winners for the 2013 Season at Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club

Prize Winners for the 2013 Season

S & J Young & Alec Duncan Memorial Greensomes - 29 September 2013.

Jim Fisher and Miss Aileen Wilson won this new greensomes format of competition to mark the end of the playing season with a fantastic nett score of 59.5. Jim and Aileen's scorecard included an eagle three at the 4th hole and a further birdie at the 14th hole playing off a handicap of 24.5 to win by 1.5 shots from Arthur MacArthur and Lewis MacLeman. The full list of results (the top 10) can be viewed from the competitions menu and results.

The Rosehaugh Medal Final - 21 September 2013.

The Rosehaugh Medal Final was played on Saturday and with five players competing for the coveted gold medal, James Fraser returned the lowest score on the day with a nett 67 to win by three shots from Gordon Gill. James' card included birdies at the 14th, 15th, 16th and 17th holes. The CSS for the day was 69.

Alliance Timber Preservation Junior Medal Final - 21 September 2013.

Euan Gill was the overall winner of the ATP Junior Medal Final for the 2013 season with a nett score of 71 playing off a handicap of 6. Euan's card included a birdie three at the 12th hole in halves of 39 and 38. The CSS for the day was 69.

ORDER OF MERIT RESULTS - 2013 SEASON.

Congratulations go to Kenny Gaittens for winning the Men's Order of Merit title for the 2013 season. With Kenny's overall consistency in the fifteen counting competitions, he won with an accumulated points total of 770 which means he scored on average 51.33 points per competition. In third place came Kevin Tough with a nett score of 67 (reducing his handicap down to 13 as a result) and this included a birdie at the 11th hole. The Kelly Open Foursomes - 4 August 2013.

This year's Kelly Open Foursomes was played somewhat tougher conditions than normal with those playing in their first round experiencing high winds throughout so it was no surprise that the scores were higher than would normally be the case. With a field totalling 108 players (54 pairs) competing in the 36-hole tournament the winners on the day and for the fourth time overall were Mike MacDonald (F & R) and Davie McIntosh (Royal Dornoch). Mike and Davie birdied four of the last 6 holes in their second round to recover well after a poor first 12 holes. Their scores of 76 and 73 proved good enough to beat the Inverness pairing of John Forbes and Bruce Thomson by one shot (75/75). In third place came Chris Gaittens and John Fair with gross scores of 80 and 72. In the handicap section the overall winners were Ewen Skinner and Kenny Gaittens with nett scores of 72 and 71. In second place were Colin Fraser and Johnston Bellshaw. To see a full list of the prize-winners please click onto the link below:-

Seniors Stableford Open - Results - July 2013

Junior Club Championship Finals - 3 July 2013.

In closely contested matches on the links at Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club, Ewan MacPherson defeated Euan Gill by 3 & 1 in the Scratch Final. This is the first time that Ewan has won the competition so congratulations go to him for this achievement.

Possibly going one better after winning the Club Championship Handicap Section at Inverness Golf Club only a week or so earlier, Andrew Howell completed a notable double by beating Calum Brindle by 2 Holes in the final. At one point Andrew was four up and Calum then played some very consistent golf to take it back to level after 16 holes. Andrew then proceeded to win the 17th hole and then also parred the last hole despite missing the green to take the title. Both winning players will be presented with special 125th anniversary medals at the annual prize-giving in October to mark their achievement.

Wednesday Sweep - 3 July 2013.

Bryan Hastie was the winner of the Wednesday Sweep on the 3rd July 2013 with an excellent nett score of 62 (playing off 21). Bryan has now taken his handicap down to 19 as a result of this score. In second place was Michael M Hasson with a nett 63 (playing off 14). Michael has also taken his handicap down to 12 as a result. In third place was Peter Rawlinson with a nett score of 66. Peter has also taken his handicap down to 12 as a result. The best gross score was recorded by Allan Cameron with a 70. The CSS for the day was 69.

Ladies Monthly Medal - 2 July 2013.

Katie Nelson was the overall winner of the Ladies Monthly Medal for the month of July with an excellent nett score of 70 (CSS 73). As a result, Katie has reduced her handicap down to 33 (33.4). In the Silver division, the lowest score returned was by Marina MacCulloch with a nett score of 73.

With the CSS for the day rising to 71, the qualifiers for the final for the 2013 season are as follows (ties to be played from 11.00 on Wednesday).

Scratch Section - Euan Gill v Ewan MacPherson (11.15) Handicap Section - Andrew Howell v Calum Brindle (11.00)

W.P. Moodie Memorial Cup - 30 June 2013.

Philip Taylor and Alistair Tait won the W.P. Moodie Memorial Cup after returning an excellent nett score (3/4 handicap - better ball) of 66 in what proved to be a very tough day for scoring with high winds affecting scores throughout the day. Club Championship Finals Day - 29 June 2013.

Allan Cameron won the Club Championship for the 2013 season and with it a special 125th anniversary medal when he defeated Peter Cameron in the final on Saturday afternoon by the score of 3 & 2. In the Semi-Final Allan beat Chris Gaittens by one hole in a match which included many birdies by both players. Peter defeated Mike MacDonald on the 15th green after scoring birdies at the 11th, 13th, 14th and 15th holes.

In the handicap section the winner for the 2013 season (also winning a 125th anniversary medal) was Kenny Gaittens. In some tough matches whereby he was giving at least 8 shots throughout the matchplay stages Kenny defeated Colin Fraser in the final by 3 & 1. Earlier in the day, Kenny had overcome David Howell on the 20th hole to reach the final.

In what was the first ever Seniors Club Championship for the Men, Robbie MacKay beat Willie Donnelly in a closely contested final on the last hole. In the handicap section of the same event the first recorded win was by Brian Hunter when he beat Lewis Patience in the final by the score of 3 & 2.

In the Ladies Club Championship Mary Galloway recorded her ninth victory in the event after beating Lynne Fraser by the score of 3 & 2 in the final. In the handicap section the winner was Cath McMartin after she beat Fiona Lackie by the score of 3 & 2.

The full list of results are on the competitions (results page) on the website.

Graham Godsman was the winner of the latest winter sweep competition with an excellent score of 78 less 13 for a nett 65 on what turned out to be a really tough day for the golfers playing in the competition especially with the rain and strong winds in the afternoon. In second place was Iain Keith with a nett 69 and in 3rd place was one of our junior players to watch out for in the future; Euan Gill with a nett 71 playing off a 3/4 handicap of 8. Gents Turkey Tourney - Stableford - 9 December 2012.

On a day of decent weather for the 70 players competing in this festive competition, the top 21 players scores were separated by a mere 3 points. On a countback, the eventual winner was Robbie MacKay with 39 points and he duly won the Christmas Hamper. In 2nd place was Mark Farquhar also with a score of 39 points and he won the Turkey and trimmings. David Robson was 3rd and won the Balvenie Malt Whisky. Gents Winter Sweep - Stableford - 1 December 2012.

Arthur MacArthur won the Gents Winter Sweep on Saturday, 1st December 2012. Whilst many people may think Arthur played 27 holes to secure his points total, he didn't and duly returned an excellent points total of 45 points. Arthur's card included birdies at the 14th and 15th holes to win by two points from his nearest challenger. In second place was Kevin Fowler (43 Points), in third place came Iain Keith (42 Points), in fourth place came Paul Moodie (41 Points) and in fifth place came Lewis MacLeman (40 Points). Ewen Lyon was the winner of the winter sweep on Saturday, 10th November 2012 with a score of 43 points. Gents Winter Sweep - Strokeplay - 28 October 2012.

Lewis recorded birdies at the 3rd, 5th, 10th, 11th, 12th, 14th, 15th and 16th holes. Robbie had birdies at the 3rd, 11th, 14th, 16th and 17th holes. PRIZEWINNERS 2012

Young Memorial Club Mixed Foursomes - 30 September 2012.

Bob Tilford and Jill Tilford won the Young Memorial Club Mixed Foursomes for the 2012 season with a nett score of 78. Despite recording two scores of 10 on the front nine at the 4th and 8th holes they both recovered very well to come back in 48 to win by virtue of a better inward half from Malcolm McArthur and Annette McArthur.

Rosehaugh Cup 1st Round & Extra Medal - 18 September 2012.

Mo Ross won the re-scheduled Rosehaugh Cup 1st Round & Extra Medal with a nett score of 77 to win by one shot from Jill Tilford. In slightly cold and unpredictable weather for all the Ladies playing in the competition it was once again reductions only in relation to the CSS for the day which rose to 75.

Maureen Wilson won the overall competition with the aggregate scores from round 1 and round 2 counting and will be presented with the trophy at the annual prize-giving in October.

Vice-Captain's Prize - 16 September 2012.

Ruaridh Gray won the Junior Vice-Captain's Prize for the 2012 season after returning a nett score of 67 which meant he won by three shots from Andrew Howell. In consistent halves of 43 and 43, Ruaridh has now reduced his handicap to 18 which gets him closer to playing in the adult competitions for next year. The prize awarded by the Club Vice-Captain will be presented at the annual prize-giving on Saturday, 27th October 2012.

Captain's Prize - 15 September 2012.

Robbie MacKay won the Captain's Prize for the season's finale competition with a nett 70 on what was a tough day for all competitors playing in the medal with high winds once again affecting scores so much that the CSS was 72 (reductions only). Robbie's score included birdies at the 6th and 18th holes to win by two shots from Lawrence MacLean.

Marjorie Moorhead Greensomes - 11 September 2012.

The pairing of Mo Ross and Sheena Dunn won the greensomes competition for the first time together with a nett score of 72.8 playing off a handicap of 18.2. With both players gelling well together on the course they won by just under three shots from Marina MacCulloch and Anne Brown.

Rosehaugh Medal Final - 9 September 2012.

Calum MacLean won the Gold Medal for the 2012 season after returning a great score of nett 67. Calum's card included birdies at the 10th, 14th and 17th holes to win by three shots from Philip Schnier. The Gold Medal will be presented at the annual prize-giving on Saturday, 27th October 2012.

Comfort Foods Junior Medal Final - 9 September 2012.

Dylan MacCulloch won this year's final with a nett score of 71 playing off a handicap of 19. Dylan's card included a birdie at the 10th hole to win by two shots from Ruaridh Gray who returned a nett 73.

Rosehaugh Medal - 8 September 2012.

Philip Schnier won the final Rosehaugh Qualifier of the 2012 season with an excellent round of gross 73 for a nett score of 66 to win by one shot from Alan Drever. Philip's round included an eagle three at the 4th and further birdies at the 7th, 11th and 16th holes.

Comfort Foods Junior Medal - 8 September 2012.

Ruaridh Gray won the final qualifier for the final which was to take place the following day with an excellent score of nett 65. Ruaridh won by 6 shots from Euan Gill who returned a nett 71 and he has now reduced his handicap down to 19 from 21.

Press Release - Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club - 5 September 2012

Ladies Monthly Medal - 4 September 2012.

Jenny Thornton won the ladies monthly medal for the month of September on what turned out to be another day of extremely high winds which were again gusting at 40mph across the course. With a winning score of nett 87, Jenny won by 3 shots from Anne MacKay. The CSS for the day was unsurprisingly 75 (Reductions Only).

St. Ann's Quaich Final - 2 September 2012.

Trish Fraser was the winner of the St. Ann's Quaich for 2012 with a nett score of 75, playing off a 12 handicap. In halves of 43 and 44, Trish won by one shot from Eileen Short.

Men's 18 Hole Open - 1 September 2012.

On what was nearly verging on the impossible for the majority of the players with the wind gusting at 45mph for the later starters in the late morning and afternoon but not taking anything away from the fact that is was not much easier in the morning, there was no surprise in the fact that the CSS for Home and Away Players was 72 (Reductions Only). The vast majority of the winning scores came from the early starters on Saturday with an excellent gross 70 from Allan Cameron winning by three shots from Davie Sanderson from Inverness (Davie won the first handicap prize in section one). The winner of the second handicap section was Gary Webster with a nett 72. Please click onto the link below to see the results:-

Morty Ross was the winner of the Wednesday Sweep for 2012 with a final round of 72 in halves of 36 and 36 for a nett 67 to win the play-off by one shot from Neil Jaffreay and by two shots from Simon Hasson. Morty's round included birdies at the 4th, 6th and 14th holes.

Friday, 31st August 2012

Colin MacArthur Memorial - 25 August 2012.

Rory MacLeman was the winner of the Colin MacArthur Memorial trophy on what turned out to be an afternoon of freak weather conditions for those playing at that time of the day in the latter parts of their round. Whilst the competition was abandoned with some of the field unable to complete their rounds due to the greens flooding, the result still stands with the competition standard scratch being 69 (reductions only). Rory's round included birdies at the 4th and 14th holes and despite a double bogey at the 16th hole, he won by two shots from his nearest challenger who was John Fair with a nett 67. Let's hope Rory fills the cup at the prize-giving in October!

Wednesday Sweep - 22 August 2012.

Neil Jaffrey won the final qualifier for the Wednesday Sweep of 2012 with a nett score of 65 which only won by virtue of a better inward half from Martin J MacKenzie. Neil's card included birdie at the 6th hole in halves of 43 and 38 and he has as a result reduced his handicap to 15 from 16. The CSS for the day was 70 with a field of 61 players competing in the final sweep of 2012. The final play-off will take place on Wednesday, 29th August 2012 with players booking their own time. Ladies Senior Stableford Open - 21 August 2012.

Third place went to Anne Smitton from the home club with a score of 31 points who secured this position by having a better inward half than Jane Harrison who is also from the home club. The closest to the pin prize went to S. Ramsay from Inverness who was 65cm from the hole with her tee shot. The CSS for the day was 73 for HOME members and 74 for all AWAY players. On what was a perfect day for scoring, Calum MacLean won the Roshaugh Medal for the month of August with a score of nett 63. Calum won by virtue of a better inward half from Chris Gaittens to qualify for the final which is to be played on Sunday, 9th September 2012. Calum's round included a birdie at the 14th hole where he came back in one under par and has now taken his handicap down to 9 from 11. Chris Gaittens shot a seven under par score of 64 despite two bogeys at the 4th and 8th holes. Chris returned birdies at the 2nd, 3rd, 6th, 10th, 12th, 13th, 14th, 16th and 18th holes. Colin High won the Sunday medal play competition in memory of John and Fraser Grigor with a nett score of 65. Colin's card included a birdie at the 14th and 17th holes to win by one shot from Andrew Brown who returned a gross 70 (playing off 4) for a nett 66. Lady Captain's Prize - 11 August 2012.

K Ann Brown won the Lady Captain's Prize for 2012 with a nett score of 73 to win by one shot from Anne MacKay. Ann's score included a birdie two at the 5th hole on what turned out to be a fantastic day for golf with the sun shining with the slight breeze from the moray firth cooling the players down. The CSS for the day was 71.

Wednesday Sweep - 8 August 2012.

On what turned out to be a perfect day for golf for all those participating in the Wednesday Sweep the CSS actually rose by one shot to 70. Alexander McDonald was the convincing winner with a nett score of 62 which included a birdie at the 11th hole in halves of 38 and 35. Morty Ross was second with a nett 65 which included birdies at the 2nd, 5th, 8th, 9th, and 15th holes. The best gross score on the day was recorded by Lewis Reid with a 69.

Ladies Monthly Medal - 7 August 2012.

Aileen Wilson won the Ladies Monthly Medal for the month of August with an excellent nett score of 64. With the CSS for the day rising to 74, Aileen now plays off a handicap of 30. Aileen birdied the 14th hole in her round. In second place overall was Ailine Drummond who had a nett 70 and has as a result reduced her handicap to 15.

The Kelly Open Foursomes - 5 August 2012.

On what turned out to be a great day for golf despite the drizzly start to the competition, Mike MacDonald and Davie McIntosh won the Kelly Open Foursomes scratch section for the 3rd time with scores of 74 and 70 to win on a better second round from Lewis Reid and Allan Cameron. Bruce Main and Chris Young won the handicap section with consistent nett scores of 68.5 and 69.5 (playing off a 9.5 handicap) despite Christopher driving in the greenside bunker at the 6th hole from the 12th tee!! In second place were Ewen Skinner and Kenny Gaittens with a nett aggregate total of 141. Following the prize-giving the Club hosted their annual auction with all proceeds going to the Highland Hospice. The figure came to just under £4000 on the day and in total through the years the Club as part of this event and other's connected to the Hospice have now raised close to £100,000 for such a worthy cause. Thanks go to all involved on the day both in the organisation of the tournament and the players who took part. Please click onto the link below to see the list of prize-winners.

Kelly Open Prize-winners - 7 August 2012

Quincentenary Cup - 3 August 2012.

Chris Gaittens won the Quincentenary Cup for the first time by recording a winning score of 42 points in Friday's competition which had a shotgun start at 5.00pm. Chris had birdies at the 3rd, 6th, 7th, 10th, 14th, 16th & 17th holes and would have been even lower but for a double bogey 6 at the 8th hole. In second place with 41 points was Alistair Tait who had birdies at the 4th, 5th and 17th holes.

Comfort Foods Junior Medal - 2 August 2012.

Dylan MacCulloch won the latest junior medal with a score of nett 64 to win on a better inward half from Scott Murray who returned a best of the day gross score of one under par 70. Dylan's round included a birdie at the 3rd and 14th holes and he has now reduced his handicap down to 21 from 23.

Wednesday Sweep - 1 August 2012.

Robert Gillett was the winner of the Wednesday Sweep this week with an excellent score of nett 65. Playing off a 14 handicap and despite running up a 7 at the 5th hole, Robert recovered to win by one shot with the aid of a birdie at the 15th hole in his round. In second place was Graham Godsman who returned a score of nett 66 which included a birdie at the 6th hole. The best gross score was recorded by Lewis Reid with a 72.

Junior Black Isle Open - 31 July 2012.

M. Schnikel from Orkney Golf Club won the Junior Black Isle Open scratch section for 2012 with an excellent score of 77 to win by three shots from Rory Franssen from Inverness Golf Club. Mst Schnikel's round included a birdie at the 6th and 10th holes. In handicap section one, the winner was J. Paterson from the St. Andrews New Golf Club. His nett score of 73 included a birdie 3 at the 11th hole and despite a triple bogey at the last hole he won his section by a large margin from his nearest challenger. In section two of the handicap section, the sponsor's son, Ruairidh Gray returned the best nett score of the day with gross score of 89 playing off a handicap of 23 which included a birdie four at the 6th hole to win the overall handicap open by six shots. The CSS for the day was 71 and as a result Ruaridh has reduced his handicap to 20.

Rosehaugh Medal - 28 July 2012.

Gary Moore, forever the runner up in competitions finally tasted victory in the Rosehaugh Medal on Saturday, 28th July 2012. His gross score of 71 (nett 66) included birdies at the 4th, 14th and 15th holes to win by two shots from Ian Reid who had a nett 68. Gary now qualifies for the final in September where the six qualifiers through the year contest a play-off for the golf medal.

Junior Bogey Competition - 27 July 2012.

New member, Tom MacLennan won the Junior Bogey Competition for 2012 with a score of 4 against the par of the course. Tom won 10 holes against the course par and lost 6, having halved two holes to win by two from Andrew Howell.

Junior Esso Shield - 26 July 2012.

Andrew Howell was the winner of the medal on Thursday, 26th July 2012 with a nett score of 64. Andrew's round included a birdie at the 10th hole in halves of 42 and 42. Andrew has now reduced his handicap down to 18.

Wednesday Sweep - 25 July 2012.

Alexander Patience was the latest winner of the Wednesday Sweep after a score of nett 63 playing off a handicap of 19. Alexander's score included birdies at the 8th and 16th holes to win by four shots from Aaron Paul who had a nett 67. In third place by virtue of a better inward half was David Elder. The best gross score of the day was recorded by Chris Gaittens with a two under par 69.

FORTROSE & ROSEMARKIE GOLF CLUB - NEWSLETTER - JULY 2012.

Golf Club Newsletter - July 2012

3-Lady Team Open - 24 July 2012.

The trio of J. Coulthard, A. Rae & N. Morrison (all from Grantown-on-Spey) won the 3-Lady Team Open for 2012 with a nett score of 58. Gross birdies at the 6th and 10th holes helped them to win by one shot from the team of Leila McWhirr, Evelyn Stewart and Aileen Wilson (all from Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club) who recorded a nett score of 59. In third place were the team from Ullapool made up of A. Ford, C. MacPherson and A. Smyrl (nett 59) who lost out by virtue of a better inward half from the local team. In 4th position were E. Hutton, E. Wallace and P. Morrison (all from Muir of Ord) with a score of 60. In 5th place were the team of Karen Mackay, Joan Darroch and Maureen Small (all from Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club) with a score of 61 who claimed 5th place by virtue of a better last hole from the team of M. Ritchie (Nairn), F. Allan (Nairn) and M. Britovsek (Nairn Dunbar). Please click onto the link below to see a full list of the results.

3-Lady Team Open Prizes - 24 July 2012

Comfort Foods Junior Medal - 23 July 2012.

Euan Gill won the latest Junior Medal with a nett score of 64 playing off a handicap of 13. As a result of Euan's score he is now eligible to play in the Gents competitions from now on which is a great achievement considering his handicap was 20 at the turn of the year. Euan's round included a birdie 3 at the 7th hole.

Rod Anderson Memorial (3 Man Team) - 22 July 2012.

Garry Keith, Andrew Brown and Maurice Brown won the Rod Anderson Memorial Trophy (3 Ball Better Ball) on Sunday, 22nd July 2012 by three shots with a nett score of 61. Their round included gross birdies on the 1st and 12th holes in what was an extremely windy day for all playing in the event. In second place with a nett score of 64 were Bruce Main, Lewis MacLeman and Jimmy Grant and in 3rd position with a nett score of 65 were Keith Patience, Willie Wilson, Robert Jack.

Rosehaugh Medal - 19 July 2012.

Paul Moodie won the re-arranged Gents Rosehaugh Medal following it's cancellation in May with a nett 65 and subsequently moved to the top of the Order of Merit for the 2012 season. Paul had a birdie at the 6th hole in halves of 39 and 42 to win by two shots from Forbes Mellis and Lewis Reid.

Wednesday Sweep - 18 July 2012.

Morty Ross won the Wednesday Sweep on what was a very poor day for golf with constant rain from early morning until the early eveing. For the 8 golfers who participated in the sweep, Morty Ross was the convincing winner of the competition with a nett score of 63 playing off a handicap of 6 (2 under par). Morty had birdies at the 5th, 6th and 16th holes in halves of 34 and 35. Second place went to Daniel Laidlaw by virtue of a better inward half with a nett 70.

Ladies Rosehaugh Cup 2nd Round & Extra Medal - 17 July 2012.

Maureen Wilson won the Ladies Rosehaugh Cup 2nd Round & Extra Medal (the first round was postponed last week due to the weather and will be played in August) with a nett score of 74. Despite running up a 10 at the 13th hole, Maureen won by one shot from Anne Gilbertson and by two from Anne Brown and Annette Jack.

Comfort Foods Junior Medal - 15 July 2012.

Euan Gill won the latest Junior Medal with an excellent score of 76 gross (nett 61). Euan is now very close to reducing his handicap down to 12 which will allow him to play in the gents competitions for the remainder of 2012. Euan recorded a birdie at the 8th hole in very consistent halves of 37 and 39. Certainly one junior who will be one to watch out for in the years to come which should act as a lot of encouragement for the juniors who have yet to obtain a handicap.

The Rutherford Cup - 14 July 2012.

Colin High was the winner of the Rutherford Cup for 2012 with a nett score of 68. Whilst the entries were affected with the Scottish Open taking place at Castle Stuart, Colin's score proved to be the winning score by virtue of a better inward half from George Leonard and Dan Patterson. Although Colin had no birdies on his card his consistent halves of 39 and 39 were good enough to take first place. Maurice Brown now leads the way in the Gents Order of Merit for 2012 having won section two with a nett 69.

Ladies Vintage Bowl - 12 July 2012.

Anne Smitton won the Ladies Vintage Bowl for 2012 with a nett score of 79. In a small field of only 7 players Anne prevailed despite running up a 13 at the 4th hole which affected her nett score considerably.

Wednesday Sweep - 11 July 2012.

Robert McIntosh won the Wednesday Sweep by a convincing margin of two shots with a nett 64 and that was despite a triple bogey 7 at the 11th hole. Robert returned halves of 38 and 39 which included birdies at the 13th and 16th holes. John Fair was second with a nett 66 playing off 5 which also included an eagle 3 at the 6th hole and birdies at the 9th, 11th and 12th holes. The best gross score was returned by Allan Cameron with a 70.

Men's Black Isle Open (36 Holes) - 7 July 2012.

Ian Wilson from Dalmahoy won the Men's Black Isle Open which was played over 36 holes for the first time on Saturday, 7th July 2012. In really poor conditions and with the rough proving an impossibility for many in the field of 88 players, Ian returned two gross 75's to win by one shot from Mike MacDonald who ran up a 9 on the 17th hole in the first round in scores of 78 and 73. Ewen Skinner from the home club won the best overall handicap aggregate for section one with a nett 73 and 70 playing off a handicap of 4. The winner in section two was one of our other local members, Duncan Bridger with a nett aggregate of 144. The CSS for Visitors was 72 R/O for both rounds and the CSS for Members was 72 R/O in round one and 72 (Counting) in round 2. Open Texas Scramble - 30 June 2012.

The team of Gary Moore, Johnston Bellshaw, Gary Ross (Strathpeffer) and Steven Bassindale won the open texas scramble with a score of gross 56 (nett 53.7). The won by 0.7 from Andy Gray, Colin Fraser, Gordon Gill and Chris Gaittens who scored 54.4. The team of Tam Cornwall, Robert McIntosh, Gary Dick and S. Jenkins (Nairn) were 3rd with a score of 55.3. In 4th place were the team of Doug Younie, Graham Godsman, Eric Brown (Inverness) and Ian Considine with a nett score of 56.3 followed by the team of Mike MacDonald, Chris Young, Neil MacDonald (Torvean) and Bruce Main who scored 56.6.

Comfort Foods Junior Medal - 29 June 2012.

Dylan MacCulloch won the Junior Medal for the month of June with a score of nett 82 in what proved to be unpredictable weather conditions for all those who played. Dylan automatically qualifies for the Junior Medal final in September of this year.

Christina MacLeod Trophy - 28 June 2012.

Maureen Wilson won the trophy for 2012 by four shots on a tough day for golf with the heavy rain forecast becoming reality and this proved to push the scores up as a result. Maureen's round of nett 74 included a birdie 3 at the 15th hole and she has now taken her handicap back down to 19. Annette Jack was second by virtue of a better inward half with a nett 78. The CSS for the day was 75 and counting.

Wednesday Sweep - 27 June 2012.

Martin MacKenzie won the Sweep with an excellent nett score of 65. Martin's round included a birdie at the 6th, 13th and 15th holes and has now reduced his handicap to 14. In a close contest, Martin won by virtue of a better inward half from Morty (Calum) Ross and Philip Schnier. Morty's round included birdies at the 1st, 11th, 14th and 15th holes for a nett 65. Philip's round included birdies at the 6th, 8th, 14th and 16th holes also for a nett 65. The best gross score went to Peter Cameron with a 70.

Ladies Ross-Sutherland Team Competition - 24 June 2012.

Tain Golf Club once again won the Ladies Ross-Sutherland Team Competition at Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club on Sunday, 24th June 2012. The team of A Ryan (81), M Smith (81), C Ross (77) and L Thompson (103) with the best three scores from the four players counting (Aggregate 239) won by 11 shots from Royal Dornoch who had an aggregate score of 250. A Bartlett (82), C. Riddell (83), D. Lloyd (85) and D McBride (96) made up the four. In the handicap section the team from Golspie 3 won their respective section. The team was made up of A. Duff (nett 72), L. Cranna (nett 83), H. Proctor (nett 88) and L. Bonner (nett 74) to win by two shots from Golspie 1.

The Gents Club Championship Semi-Finals & Finals - 23 June 2012.

Allan Cameron won the Club Championship scratch section for 2012 after beating Lewis Reid 3 & 2 in the final. Allan Cameron had earlier beaten Chris Gaittens by one hole in a closely fought semi-final match in the morning and Lewis Reid defeated Mike MacDonald in another close match on the 17th green. Kevin Fowler won the Handicap title after beating Steven Bassindale by 3 & 2. In the morning's semi finals Kevin beat Willie Donnelly Jnr 5 & 4 and Steven Bassindale defeated Willie Wilson by 4 & 3.

The Ladies Club Championship Finals - 23 June 2012.

There were two new winners of the Club Championship for 2012 in the Ladies Section. The winner of the scratch title was Janette Kennedy-Spence who won the final by 6 & 5 against Marsha Fraser. The winner of the Handicap title was the current ladies Captain, Joan Darroch who also won by the score of 5 & 4 against Annette McArthur. Congratulations to both players on winning their respective competitions and well done to Annette and Marsha for making the final.

The Chapman Trophy - 22 June 2012.

Chris Gaittens and John Fair won the Chapman Trophy which is played in a very different format from the normal foursomes or greensomes competitions for the first time with a score of 63.5 to win by 1.5 shots once the handicaps have been taken into consideration from Jimmy Smith and Martin J. MacKenzie. Chris and John had birdies at the 2nd, 3rd, 4th, 5th, 14th, 15th and 16th holes in what was an impressive score under very tricky scoring conditions due to a strong easterly wind.

Wednesday Sweep - 20 June 2012.

Robbie Kernahan won the Wednesday sweep this week with an excellent nett score of 65. Robbie's round included an eagle three at the par 5, 6th hole and a birdie three at the 15th hole in halves of 38 and 40 to win by three shots from James Fraser and Morty Ross who had nett scores of 68. The best gross score went to Robbie MacKay who scored a 73 after coming back in a one under par 34.

Ladies Charity Stableford - 19 June 2012.

Jenny Thornton won the Ladies Charity Stableford which took the form of a shotgun start this year at 5.30pm with a stableford score of 36 points. Jenny's round included a birdie two at the 5th hole. In second place was Eileen Short with a score of 35 points on a great evening for golf on the links.

Gents Club Championship - Quarter-Finals - 17 June 2012.

Where players playing on Saturday in the qualifiers were unlucky with the weather the opposite was the case on Sunday for the Quarter Final Matches. On a perfect day for golf the top 8 scratch and handicap qualifiers from the previous day's golf battled it out to reach the semi-finals which would take place on Saturday, 23rd June 2012. In the Scratch Section, Lewis Reid won a closely fought match against Corin Stewart on the 18th hole. Chris Gaittens won against his father, Kenny Gaittens (on fathers day too!) by 4 & 3. Mike MacDonald won his match against Michael Manson by 6 & 5 and Allan Cameron won his match against Andrew Brown 2 & 1. For the first time in a number of years the top four scratch qualifiers will meet in the Semi-Finals with Lewis Reid playing Mike MacDonald and Chris Gaittens playing Allan Cameron. In the Handicap Section, Steven Bassindale won a closely fought encounter with Willie Donnelly on the 17th green and will now play Willie Wilson in the Semi-Final on Saturday after Willie beat David Douglas by the score of 3 & 1. In the remaining Quarter-Final matches, Kevin Fowler defeated Malcolm McArthur 2 & 1 and he will now play against Willie Donnelly Jnr after he won his match on the last hole against Alistair MacIntyre.

For all the results of the matches played on Sunday, please visit the results page for a full breakdown with tee-times for the Semi-Finals and Finals which will take place on Saturday, 23rd June 2012.

Ladies Club Championship - Semi-Finals - 17 June 2012.

On a great day for golf as opposed to the previous day (Men's Club Championship Qualifying Rounds) when it was a case of keeping your score down, the semi-final matches for the Ladies Club Championship took place. In the Handicap Section, the Lady Captain, Joan Darroch won the first semi-final match against the former Lady Captain, K Ann Brown by 5 & 3. In the second Semi-Final Match, Annette McArthur won through against Cath McMartin by 6 & 5. The Ladies Final for the Handicap Section will take place on Saturday, 23rd June 2012 at 13.15. In the Scratch Section Janette Kennedy-Spence prevailed in her match against the current Lady Vice-Captain, Loraine Nixon by 3 & 2 and Marsha Fraser reached the final of the Scratch Section for the first time after defeating Kay Bisset on the 17th green. The Ladies Scratch Final will also take place on Saturday with the match starting at 13.30.

Details of all the matches played and the timings for the final can be accessed from the competitions page on the website then by clicking onto the results section.

Gents Club Championship Qualifying (36 Holes) - 16 June 2012.

On a really tough day for golf on the Links, good scoring was really hard to come by as the strong easterly wind remained apparent throughout the day. With the CSS for both rounds being 72 (reductions only) most players in the field were very happy to get in after their rounds and not see their handicaps go up after battling the elements throughout the day. Top position in the Scratch Section went to Chris Gaittens with a gross aggregate score of 148 (6 over par) and he was closely followed by Lewis Reid (148), Mike MacDonald (149) and Allan Cameron (149). In the Handicap Section, top honours went to Steven Bassindale with a nett aggregate score of 148. Steven was closely followed by Malcolm McArthur (149), Willie Donnelly Jnr (149) and Willie Wilson (150). The top 8 scratch aggregate scores and the top 8 handicap aggregate scores qualified for the Quarter Final on Sunday, 17th June 2012. Please see the report above.

Ladies Club Championship - Round 3 - 14 June 2012.

With the weather experienced by the golfers on the course somewhat tough to say the least with a strong easterly wind, the chances of a good score were few and far between which was reflected in the CSS rising to 74 (reductions only). The qualifiers for the Semi-Finals of the Scratch Section for 2012 were Janette Kennedy-Spence, Kay Bisset, Marsha Fraser and Loraine Nixon. In the Handicap Section the qualifiers were K. Ann Brown, Annette McArthur, Cath McMartin and Joan Darroch. The Semi-Finals are to be played on Sunday morning (17th) and the Finals are to be be played on Saturday, 23rd June 2012. Click onto the link below to see the semi-final line-ups for 2012.
