Wednesday Sweep - 13 June 2012.

Aaron Paul won the Wednesday Sweep with a nett score of 66 playing off a handicap of 14. As a result Aaron has reduced his handicap down to 13 after beating the CSS which rose to 70 by 4 shots. His round included a birdie 3 at the 14th hole. In second position losing out by virtue of the better inward half was Roddie MacPherson and in third place was Andy Gray with a nett 67 (again by virtue of a better inward half) which included birdies at the 6th, 7th, 9th and 14th holes.

Ladies Club Championship - Round 2 - 12 June 2012.

The best nett score on the day came from Annette McArthur with a nett 72. Despite a 10 at the 4th hole, Annette was pretty consistent on the remaining holes played through that morning. The highlight of the day was the first ever hole in one recorded by Jill Tilford on the 5th hole (details below). The CSS remained the same for the day at 72. Players competing in the final round on Thursday will play off the same handicaps as they did on Tuesday, 12th June 2012. The qualifiers for the Semi-Finals of the Scratch and Handicap Sections (to take place on Sunday) will be known on Friday morning.

Hole in One Achievement at the 5th Hole - 12 June 2012.

Jill Tilford scored her first ever hole in one at the 5th hole using a hybrid golf club (23 degrees) at Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club. The hole in one was achieved in the Ladies Club Championship 2nd Round on Tuesday, 12th June 2012. Jill was partnered by Annette McArthur.

W.P. Moodie Memorial Cup - 10 June 2012.

Colin Fraser and Gordon Gill won the W.P. Moodie Memorial Cup (fourball better ball format) for the first time with a nett score of 61. Gross birdies at the 6th, 10th, 13th, 14th and 17th in halves of 33 and 28 ensured that both players won the competition by two shots from Willie Wilson and Keith Patience. I am sure the trophy was filled up on Sunday night!

Ross-Shire County Championship - 9 June 2012.

Allan Cameron of Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club won the Ross-Shire County Championship for the first time with scores of 69 & 72. Allan won by five shots from Lyle McAlpine (68 & 78) who had won the competition for the previous two years. In tough conditions for the field of 28 players (seven of which did not go out for the second round) the scores posted by Allan were more than good enough to beat the other players playing in the competition on the day.

T.S.H. Burns Memorial Cup - 8 June 2012.

Kenny Gaittens and Ewen Skinner won the greensomes competition with a score of nett 70 in what was tough scoring for all players who participated on Friday evening. Their scorecard included a birdie at the 2nd, 3rd, 8th and 15th holes to win by 0.25 from their nearest challengers who were Lewis Patience and Jimmy Grant.

Jack MacKay Seniors - 7 June 2012.

Dan Patterson won the Jack MacKay trophy for 2012 with an excellent score of nett 67 in somewhat breezy playing conditions. Despite starting with a double bogey 6, Dan steadied the ship and put together a very consistent round of golf which included a birdie at the 10th hole to reduce his playing handicap down to 11. Maurice Brown finished in second place two shots behind Dan with a nett 69 and also reduced his handicap to 16 as a result of the CSS rising to 71 for the day.

Gents Wednesday Sweep - 6 June 2012.

Whilst many players playing in the sweep experienced some persistent rain, the winning score on the day came from one of the newer members of the Club in Ewen Lyon with a nett 65 playing off a handicap of 27 (this has now been reduced to 25). Ewen's round included a birdie 3 at the 13th hole and in the end he won by two shots from Aaron Paul who returned a nett 67 and by three shots from Neil Jaffrey who despite an 8 at the 10th hole came home with a nett 68.

Ladies Club Championship Round 1 & Monthly Medal - 5 June 2012.

Marsha Fraser won the Ladies Monthly Medal for June with a nett score of 66 playing off a handicap of 21. In halves of 44 & 43 she won by 6 shots from her nearest challenger, Lynne Fraser who returned a score of gross 77 playing off a handicap of 5. The second qualifying round of the Ladies Club Championship will take place on Tuesday, 12th June 2012.

Gents Rosehaugh Medal - 3 June 2012.

Aaron Paul won the Rosehaugh Medal on Sunday, 3rd June with a nett score of 65 playing off a handicap of 16 (now reduced to 15). Aaron won the competition by four shots from his nearest challenger who was Robbie MacKay who had a gross 73 (nett 69). Aaron's round included a birdie three at the 14th hole in an inward half of 37 to run out a convincing winner and will now go forward to play for the Gold Medal in a play-off in September once the six finalists are known.

Comfort Foods Junior Medal - 1 June 2012.

Euan Gill won the Junior Medal for the month of June with a nett score of 69 playing off a handicap of 18. Despite an 8 at the 3rd hole, Euan won by two shots from Scott Murray who returned a nett score of 71.

Gents Wednesday Sweep - 30 May 2012.

Davie Tuach won the Wednesday Sweep on 30 May 2012 with a nett score of 66 playing off a handicap of 9. Davie's round included a birdie at the 6th and 14th holes in halves of 38 and 37 and has as a result reduced his handicap down to 7.9. Davie won the competition by two shots from Bryan Hastie who returned a nett score of 68 and by three shots from Brian MacKenzie who returned a score of nett 69.

Re-Scheduled Rosehaugh Medal - NEW DATE!

Following on from the cancellation of the Gents Rosehaugh Medal on Sunday, 13th May 2012 due to the high winds (with golf balls blowing off the greens) the new date for the competition will be on Thursday, 19th July 2012. Times are available on the sheets from 09.00-10.30, from 13.00-14.00 and also from 16.30-18.10.

MacKeddie Cup Foursomes - 29 May 2012.

Mo Ross & Jeanette Arthur won the MacKeddie Cup Foursomes for 2012 with a nett score of 77.5 despite a seven at the last hole to win by 0.5 from their nearest rivals who were Aline Drummond and Anne Brown. Despite the 7 on their card at the last a consistent back nine contributed to the pairing winning the competition for the first time.

Sir Hector Munro Club Mixed Foursomes - 27 May 2012.

Malcolm McArthur & Mrs Annette McArthur won the Sir Hector Munro Club Mixed Foursomes with a nett score of 75.5 playing off a handicap of 18.5. The key to the round was a birdie 3 at the 14th hole to win by half a shot from John Gill and Mrs Jenny Gill who returned a nett score of 76 despite running up a 10 at the 2nd hole.

Seniors Stableford Open - 24 May 2012.

Garry Cameron won the Seniors Stableford Open with an excellent total of 44 points on what was a perfect day for golf for the 134 competitors in the field. Garry had birdies at the 3rd, 11th, 13th and 14th holes and has reduced his handicap from 12 to 10. Whilst Garry Cameron won section one (scratch to 15 handicaps) an ex-member, Kevin Carpenter now a member at Inverness won the 16-28 section with a score of 40 points to win on a better inward half from one of our own members, William McWhirr. The CSS for the day despite the perfect scoring conditions rose to 70 for both home and away players. Click onto the link below to see the prize-winners for 2012.

Philip Schiner won the Wednesday Sweep on 23 May 2012 with a nett score of 67 playing off a 7 handicap. Philip's round included a birdie at the 1st, 4th, 5th and 16th holes. Ladies Thistle Brooch - 22 May 2012.

Gents Chanonry Open - 19 May 2012.

Congratulations go to Ian Duff who won the Chanonry Open for 2012 with a nett score of 68. The CSS for the day rose to 70. Ian's score included a birdie at the 7th hole in halves of 39 and 41 to win by one shot from John Lackie (69) and Paul Moodie (69).

Gents Shotgun Foursomes - 18 May 2012.

A total of 50 players played in the first shotgun foursomes of the season with a 6.00pm start. The overall winners were Davie Tuach and Stephen McGregor with nett score of 69.5 playing off a handicap of 8.5. Their score included a birdie 4 at the 6th and a birdie 3 at the 14th hole. Stephen and Davie won on a countback from the pairings of Lewis Reid and John Fair and the oldest pairing in the competition - Philip Taylor and Alistair Tait.

Gents Wednesday Sweep - 16 May 2012.

Simon Hasson won the Wednesday Sweep on 16 May 2012 with a nett score of 67 playing off a 23 handicap. Simon has as a result of his score reduced his handicap to 22. The CSS for the day was 71. For the second week in succession Martin McLaren (now in his 85th year) scored a gross 86 to claim second place - a fantastic achievement Martin - well done. The highlight of Martin's round was a birdie two at the 5th hole.

Ladies Una Gill Trophy (3-Lady Team) - 15 May 2012.

The winning score this year came from Joan Darroch (Lady Captain), Loraine Nixon (Lady Vice-Captain) and Karen Mackay with a nett score of 64 in this three ball better ball competition. Karen birdied the 13th hole and the 15th hole for nett 2's as part of her own score which went a long way to the team claiming a two shot victory over their nearest rivals who came in with a nett 66.

Rosehaugh Medal - 13 May 2012.

Due to adverse weather conditions (with golf balls blowing off the green due to the high winds) this competition was cancelled and will be re-scheduled at the earliest opportunity with members being informed by e-mail when a new date is known.

Lady Presidents Prize & Monthly Medal - 12 May 2012.

Jeanette Arthur returned a score of nett 76 to win the Lady Presidents Prize for 2012 and the Monthly Medal for May with a nett score of 76. Jeanette also took 0.5 from her handicap. Due to the high scoring in this competition the CSS was 75 (reductions only).

Gents Wednesday Sweep - 9 May 2012.

James Stewart won the first Wednesday Sweep of the 2012 season with a nett score of 64 playing off a handicap of 16. James' score included a birdie at the 6th hole and he won by one shot from Willam M Jack and Alexander McDonald who returned nett scores of 65. Lewis Reid shot a three under par 68 which included four birdies an eagle three at the 6th hole and an eagle 2 at the 15th hole to win the best overall gross prize.

Ladies St. Ann's Quaich 2nd Round & Extra Medal - 8 May 2012.

On another good day for golf on the links, Trish Fraser won the overall medal play competition with a nett score of 71 (playing off 12 - Trish has now reduced her handicap down to 11.6). Anne Brown finished second with an overall nett score of 72 and has reduced her handicap down to 24 from her original 25 handicap at the start of the day. The CSS for the day rose to 75 (Counting).

Open Mixed Greensomes - Sunday, 6 May 2012.

On a great day for golf, Mr R Murray (Royal Dornoch) and Mrs W. Murray (Royal Dornoch) won first prize in the scratch section with an excellent round of gross 76 to win by two shots. The Handicap Winners for Section One (Scratch-17) were Mr Hamish MacCulloch and Mrs Marina MacCulloch both members at Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club with a nett score of 67. The winners of Section 2 (Handicaps 17.5-32) with a great score of nett 62.5 were Mr Malcolm McArthur and Mrs Annette McArthur who were also home club members.

Ladies St. Ann's Quaich 1st Round - 1 May 2012.

On a sunny, but slightly breezy day for great scoring on the Links, Anne Brown won the St. Ann's Quaich 1st Round with a nett score of 76. As a result of the high scoring the CSS for the day rose to 75 (Reductions Only).

Rees-McIntosh - 28 April 2012 - Gents & Ladies.

Paul Moodie won his second title of the year whilst scoring 41 points and winning by virtue of a better inward half in the Rees-McIntosh stableford competition. Paul birdied the 12th hole in his excellent round. Anne Brown won the Ladies section competition by scoring 32 points. The full list of results can be viewed from the Competitions section on the website.

Ladies Coronation Foursomes - 24 April 2012.

Congratulations go to Jenny Thornton and Marina MacCulloch for winning the LGU Coronation Foursomes qualifier at Fortrose & Rosemarkie Golf Club. Their winning score by three shots puts them into one of 16 area finals in the UK. Should they win the area final in August they will then have the chance to compete in the grand final which will take place in St. Andrews on Monday, 24 September 2012. The winning pair in the grand final will be invited to play in the Ricoh Women’s British Open Pro-Am in 2013.

W. Young Memorial Trophy - 22 April 2012.

Despite a double bogey on the 13th and two dropped shots over the final three holes, Alistair MacIntyre was the convincing winner of the W. Young Memorial Trophy, returning a nett score of 64 playing off a handicap of 10. Alistair recorded birdies at the 4th, 6th, 8th and 15th in halves of 35 & 39 and has now reduced his playing handicap to 8. The CSS for the day was 71.

Ladies Monthly Medal - 21 April 2012.

On a tough day for scoring on the Links, Aline Drummond won the Ladies Monthly Medal for the month of April with a nett score of 77. The CSS for the day rose to 75.

The Black Isle Open Foursomes - 14/15 April 2012.

Mike MacDonald (F & R) and Chris Gaittens (F & R) retained the Black Isle Open Foursomes title they won for the first time in 2011 by beating five time champions Neil Hampton (Royal Dornoch) and Colin Taylor (Kinloss) in the final of the Scratch Section after winning by 2 holes in their match-play tie. Marc Windsor (F & R) and Jared Simpson (Nairn) won the Handicap title for the first time by beating Bruce Main (F & R) and Chris Young (F & R) 4 & 3 in the final.
